    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer4036958228283236031">The Interludes is an anthology of stand alone stories that exist between Book #2 (Afterimage) and Book #4 (Fade) of the In The Company of Shadows series. This anthology contains key plot points and major development of characters and relationships that cannot be missed.<br/><br/>In the Company of Shadows series description:<br/><br/>Years after the bombs of WWIII have changed the physical and</span>
  <span id="freeText4036958228283236031" style="display:none">The Interludes is an anthology of stand alone stories that exist between Book #2 (Afterimage) and Book #4 (Fade) of the In The Company of Shadows series. This anthology contains key plot points and major development of characters and relationships that cannot be missed.<br /><br />In the Company of Shadows series description:<br /><br />Years after the bombs of WWIII have changed the physical and political landscape, the Agency ruthlessly works behind the scenes to take down rebel groups that threaten the current government. Their goals justify all means. Hsin Liu Vega (Sin) is their most efficient and deadly assassin ever. However, he tends to go off on unauthorized killing sprees and somehow his assigned partners all end up dead under suspicious circumstances. That is why the Agency has had him locked up in a box on the fourth floor for years. But now they think it is time to put the psychopath back in the field. With a new partner.<br /><br />Boyd's mother, a high ranking Agency official, volunteers her teenage son for the position. Boyd is not afraid of death. In fact, his life has been such an endless cycle of apathy and despair for the last few years that he'd welcome it.<br /><br />Can these two broken men form an efficient partnership? Can they learn to trust anyone, let alone each other? Sin doesn't give a fuck about the Agency, or the androgynous boy who holds the remote to the shock collar that is supposed to control him.<br /><br />On the other hand, Boyd is strangely unafraid of the man everyone calls 'monster' and Sin seems reluctant to let his keeper get himself killed on any missions. Yet.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4036958228283236031" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

    <div id=buyButtonContainer class="uitext buttons buyableFeature u-marginTopXSmall u-paddingBottomXSmall u-bottomGrayBorder" data-book-id=10506860 >

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1816742862" />
    <a title="Deborah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24383684-deborah"><img alt="Deborah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515068567p2/24383684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1816742862?book_show_action=true">Dec 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deborah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deborah" href="/user/show/24383684-deborah">Deborah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24383684-deborah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1816742862" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16793701911494050960">I’ve just finished my re-read and this book, this series is the reason why I rarely give 5*<br/><br/>Original Review.<br/><br/>Absolutely brilliant.<br/>I really struggled with Afterimage simply because I wanted Sin and Boyd together, facing life head on but Boyd had other ideas and drove me crazy to the extent I stopped thinking of him as Boyd and starting to think of him as Selfish Bastard instead.<br/>This book is different from the rest and to certain point it provided relief from the emotional drain of Afterimage but no</span>
  <span id="freeText16793701911494050960" style="display:none">I’ve just finished my re-read and this book, this series is the reason why I rarely give 5*<br /><br />Original Review.<br /><br />Absolutely brilliant.<br />I really struggled with Afterimage simply because I wanted Sin and Boyd together, facing life head on but Boyd had other ideas and drove me crazy to the extent I stopped thinking of him as Boyd and starting to think of him as Selfish Bastard instead.<br />This book is different from the rest and to certain point it provided relief from the emotional drain of Afterimage but not as much as I'd expected because I was still upset with Boyd.<br />This is a collection featuring most of the main characters and like the rest of this series it's truly amazing and who would have thought after all he's done I'd end up loving Emilio, not me that's for sure but I did in fact it's hard not to love him and he provides humour sometimes in the most unexpected places.<br />Despite the fact that I really disliked Boyd in the previous book and I love Sin unconditionally I still wanted them together and therefore<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ivan annoyed the shit out of me, I didn't want Ivan, didn't like him and despite the total unfairness of it all I didn't want them to have sex, I was gutted when they did and even more gutted when Boyd continued to piss about, I mean seriously claim your man and cut the crap <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Some of these made difficult reading, who am I kidding most of these made difficult reading. I'm now in the position of absolutely dreading the next book. The reviews are brilliant and I've no doubt by the end I'll agree with them and love it like I have with the others but....<br />It's a huge but. <br />Boyd has been given a mission and it's awful and don't know if I can bear to read it. I will of course I'm just being drama queen but it's going to make for a difficult read and I need to point out again that I hate the Agency with a passion and it's completely crazy that they spend all this time and money developing really great Agents to them treat them like they're worthless holding termination over their heads at every turn.<br />This collection yet again took me through the whole spectrum of emotions and for a while I was happy but then Boyd gets his bloody mission and I'm back to square one. <br />There's so much here and so many more questions are thrown up, this is probably the best series I've read, it's totally addictive and emotional and it's taken over my life to the extend where when I'm not actually reading about these characters I'm thinking about them you could say I'm obsessed.<br />I'm dreading the end of this series, how am I ever going to manage without these guys?</span>
  <a data-text-id="16793701911494050960" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14693317759617598943"><br/><a href='http://s1354.beta.photobucket.com/user/syleegurl13/media/ICoS/14c5aa6a-37d3-422e-b56c-3f0203b3fc4e_zps2f8ab8ca.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/>Me at the first 10% - "I HATE THIS BOOK SO MUCH"<br/>Me by the end - "I LOVE THIS BOOK SO MUCH"<br/><br/>And thus, my ICoS journey continues...<br/><br/>I should say that I think Sonny & Ais are masters in laying out a series. Yes, the books can be long/dense/frustrating. But they took 1500 pages of intense reading to reel you in with Evenfall. They continued on with 1000 pages of torment and destruction in Afterimages. And then, after starting you off with a slap to the face just to make sure you’re still with them</span>
  <span id="freeText14693317759617598943" style="display:none"><br><a href="http://s1354.beta.photobucket.com/user/syleegurl13/media/ICoS/14c5aa6a-37d3-422e-b56c-3f0203b3fc4e_zps2f8ab8ca.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403350i/784683.jpg" alt=" photo 14c5aa6a-37d3-422e-b56c-3f0203b3fc4e_zps2f8ab8ca.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Me at the first 10% - "I HATE THIS BOOK SO MUCH"<br>Me by the end - "I LOVE THIS BOOK SO MUCH"<br><br>And thus, my ICoS journey continues...<br><br>I should say that I think Sonny &amp; Ais are masters in laying out a series. Yes, the books can be long/dense/frustrating. But they took 1500 pages of intense reading to reel you in with Evenfall. They continued on with 1000 pages of torment and destruction in Afterimages. And then, after starting you off with a slap to the face just to make sure you’re still with them…they progress the story, with great satisfaction, and at such a perfect pace with Interludes.<br><br>I loved this book. What a treat.<br><br>Some of it was PAINFUL.<br>Some of it was INTRIGUING.<br>Some of it was BLISSFUL.<br>Some of it was HILARIOUS.<br>Some of it was INFURIATING.<br>Some of it was TWISTED.<br>Some of it was BEAUTIFUL.<br><br>And ALL of it was FANTASTIC. And some of the BEST dialogue between characters in various scenes ever! (…oh…and <b>
  <u>VERMONT</u>
</b>…*sigh* *happy face*…just sayin’)<br><br>I wish it could end here…but alas, cliffhangers will not allow this…<br><br>Ugh…onward to Fade. <br><br><u>After book 3:</u><br><br>Boyd – bearable<br>Hsin – Love…(no other word will do)<br>Kassian – hmph…*rolling eyes*<br>Emilio – pure comedy<br>Zach – let’s remove that stick up your ass, ok?<br>Ivan – Bizzaro-Boyd was necessary<br>Ryan – MINE!...mine, mine, MINE!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15437795299818822862">I know many are removing their ratings and reviews of all the books they have read, written by Santino Hassell, in light of his despicable behavior. I have deleted my ratings from all Santino books I have read, because I too am shocked and appalled!!! I won't do it with the ICOS series though. I am gonna be honest here and say, that this series is one of the best I have ever read, and I am sure Ais played a big part in my enjoyment. As far as I know, Ais had nothing to do with all that has happe</span>
  <span id="freeText15437795299818822862" style="display:none">I know many are removing their ratings and reviews of all the books they have read, written by Santino Hassell, in light of his despicable behavior. I have deleted my ratings from all Santino books I have read, because I too am shocked and appalled!!! I won't do it with the ICOS series though. I am gonna be honest here and say, that this series is one of the best I have ever read, and I am sure Ais played a big part in my enjoyment. As far as I know, Ais had nothing to do with all that has happend. Until I hear otherwise, my ratings and reviews for this series, will stay up. I am sorry for those who might not agree with me on this. I would also like to say that I am so sorry for all of you who have been hurt....my heart goes out to all of you ;) xoxo<br><br><br>Re-read 7/14/17....damn but it seems that these books are even better the second time around. I also feel a bit less angry than I did the first time... Still made me yell and cry and rant though LOL :P<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/9051126_zpsfbahhm7l.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

So much so, that when I sleep I even dream about Sin and Boyd and their band of merry men :D<br><br>This book was a much easier read. It was still emotional en I still got frustrated with most characters, multiple times, but it also had a lot of love and laughter in it. There were however also a lot of parts that angered me :( but it was all part of the story. <br>A story I seriously love, so I excepted all the bad and frustrating parts that came with it.<br><br>Boyd especially drove me crazy in this one. I hated a lot of what he did. I was disgusted with him a few times, but in the end I couldn't help but love him and I think I always will. <br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/200_s_zpsdnprgmyv.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2780757393" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7898857751362425418">After the jarring roller-coaster ride that the previous book put me through, I was in urgent need of a break. Something lighter that wouldn't try to shred my feelings every step of the way. I almost managed the switch to Netflix... for about a minute, or two... until I decided to sneak <em>juuuuuuuuust</em> a small peak into the third book. And the rest is history.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1556220332ra/27413663.gif' alt='defeated sigh' width='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was expecting to be hit with yet another bout of depression, but somehow ended up laughing hysterically right from the first few pages. No o</span>
  <span id="freeText7898857751362425418" style="display:none">After the jarring roller-coaster ride that the previous book put me through, I was in urgent need of a break. Something lighter that wouldn't try to shred my feelings every step of the way. I almost managed the switch to Netflix... for about a minute, or two... until I decided to sneak <em>juuuuuuuuust</em> a small peak into the third book. And the rest is history.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1556220332ra/27413663.gif" alt="defeated sigh" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was expecting to be hit with yet another bout of depression, but somehow ended up laughing hysterically right from the first few pages. No one can resist Emilio Vega's charms. He can waltz in on Carhart having sex, nonchalantly wait for the guy to finish, then brazenly demand to move in... and I'd just nod, and point out the be-- er couch. Definitely the couch.<br>Logically, I knew I should've been appalled on the woman's behalf, but all I could manage was some baffled gaping, followed by manic laughter. <strong>*swoons*</strong><br><br>The Interludes were <em>juuuust</em> the thing to get me out of the post-<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8164593.Afterimage__In_the_Company_of_Shadows___2_" title="Afterimage (In the Company of Shadows, #2) by Ais" rel="nofollow noopener">Afterimage</a> blues: they were funny, bitter-sweet, cute, occasionally heart-wrenchingly painful, but most of all simply... <strong>perfect</strong>. It was like my favorite feel-good fanfiction, that gives a brief glimpse into the characters' more domestic activities. It even let me indulge in "forbidden" fantasies, but most importantly: it provides irrefutable proof that the authors <em>always</em> know best.<br><br>In other words: for all that I may find Boyd and Kass totally sizzling together, <em>nothing</em> compares to the perfection that is Boyd and Hsin as an OTP.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1556220530ra/27413670.gif" alt="excited fidgeting" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wish I had stopped to savor this book more, instead of jumping head-first into the sequel.<br><br><strong>Score: 5/5 stars</strong><br><br>This was hands down my <em>favorite</em> of the four (five?) ICoS books. For all that it took me 4 days to get through, by the end of it I felt like not even a day has passed. I honestly have <em>no idea</em> what else I was up to during the reading process... I mean, my time sheet is proof that I must've gone to work at some point, so that's a good thing. Hopefully. <strong>*cringes*</strong><br><br>=================<br>Review of vol1 of book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2159457466" rel="nofollow noopener">Evenfall: Volume 1: Director's Cut</a><br>Review of vol2 of book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2160490850" rel="nofollow noopener">Evenfall: Volume 2: Director's Cut</a><br>Review of book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2750521621" rel="nofollow noopener">Afterimage</a><br>Review of book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2785238925" rel="nofollow noopener">Fade</a></span>

I couldn't understand Boyd, I could not see the truth in his stateme</span>
  <span id="freeText1578044904456601414" style="display:none">Another <b> BIGGEST 5 STARS </b> for a book that completely consumed me!!! I LOVED every second, every word, every page, every scene! EVERYTHING!!!<br><br><b> SIN </b> - still awesome!!!<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465036222i/19305846._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b> Boyd </b> - well he didn't do something BIG like I would have wanted him tot do... after everything in the second book, but he did loved Sin and was not afraid to tell him how much.<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465036222i/19305847._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8164593.Afterimage__In_the_company_of_shadows___2_" title="Afterimage (In the company of shadows, #2) by Santino Hassell" rel="nofollow noopener">Afterimage</a> was absolutely great, but it was also full of angst and made me ache so bad! I couldn't understand Boyd, I could not see the truth in his statements and it broke my heart to see Sin suffer so much... <br><br>I kind of loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10506860.The_Interludes__In_the_Company_of_Shadows___3_" title="The Interludes (In the Company of Shadows, #3) by Santino Hassell" rel="nofollow noopener">The Interludes</a> more because the attraction between Sin and Boyd was so intense... the way they had to hide their feelings and work on their problems! <br><br><i> I don't really know how but I love this series more and more!!! </i><br><br>I was sure they will get back together but I knew it will take time. <b> And it took too much time for my taste! </b> I was craving for any scenes in which they were together and I had to wait so much!<br>I loved "Captain America". Ivan not so much, but it wasn't his fault I just didn't want Sin with anyone else. <br><br>Kassian had something ... sweet about himself. I loved his personality, I enjoyed his jokes, the way he made Boyd relax. I think it was a good experience for Boyd. Maybe it opened his eyes more about Sin and the way Sin made him feel everything. <b> And I really loved a very jealous Boyd!!!!! </b> <br><br>Also, I enjoyed their trip alone a lot and wanted, just like them, to always be like that... <br>The end of the book surprised me. I am so sorry for Emilio and Carhart and can't wait to read MORE!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1578044904456601414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_574119244" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/574119244" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4844873-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1299680097p2/4844873.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/574119244?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/4844873-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer574119244" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15749122626276730285"><br/>***Spoilers Ahead***<br/><br/>Interludes is book three In the Company of Shadows series. A reading addiction and journey that has crawled under my skin, wrapped around my reading heart and soul, and squeezed. Anger and tears. Rage and love. The characters, world, chemistry, and conspiracy have completely sucked me in. I couldn’t stop reading now if I tried! Consumed, addicted, and *twitching* right now because I’m not reading. <br/><br/>I might as well get my confession out now—I struggled with the change of style </span>
  <span id="freeText15749122626276730285" style="display:none"><br />***Spoilers Ahead***<br /><br />Interludes is book three In the Company of Shadows series. A reading addiction and journey that has crawled under my skin, wrapped around my reading heart and soul, and squeezed. Anger and tears. Rage and love. The characters, world, chemistry, and conspiracy have completely sucked me in. I couldn’t stop reading now if I tried! Consumed, addicted, and *twitching* right now because I’m not reading. <br /><br />I might as well get my confession out now—I struggled with the change of style with this book. The switch from a flowing narrative to short stories threw me off at first. I went from getting every detail in words and thoughts to flashes and jumps in time and action. The holes left me longing for more. Once I adjusted to the format though, I embraced the style full force. The way the stories changed in tone, voices, and views began to lure me deeper and deeper into the cast of characters and twists &amp; turns. Giving just enough information to make me *need* and thirst for more! Read, flip, click, click, click! The pain, loss, and longing felt reinforced and deeper with each story. Emotions swirled, pulsed, and punched at me. Hands in fists. Nails digging into my palm. Tears. Pain. Relief. Pride. Love. Hell…every emotion imaginable flew out of me at one point or another! <br /><br /><b>“Despite everything I’ve done and what everyone has said about me, I’ve realized lately that somehow I’ve stayed more human inside than a lot of other people on the compound and I won’t compromise that for anyone when it comes to fighting for something I believe is right.”</b><br /> <br />Time to step back, examine, and find ourselves in this world is rare. Find our strengths as individuals. Find a sense of stability. Feel secure in our own skins. Hsin and Boyd needed space and gave each other that time. And I love them even more for it. This leg of the journey was such a powerful blend of frustration and joy. Separate paths developed allowing readers to see Boyd gain confidence in himself and his skills while Hsin began to reach out and open up to people. Both men began to feel so much stronger to me. My heart pretty much popped with glowing pride and joy when Sin began to make friends. But the magnetic pull between Sin and Boyd still pulsed under the actions and words. As they struggled to find a new comfortable ground as partners and friends again, a new energy pushed the story along with hope and strength. Painful and awkward at times, but necessary. I loved their time apart. They needed it. Their individual battles pulled a dazzling mix of love and fear out of me. So happy for new friends and skills, but so scared they wouldn’t find their way back to each other. <br /><br />My favorite part of this book was the Hong Kong mission. It had it all! A city to explore, new characters, action, history, humor, and moments to get lost in. Moments of comfortable silence and talk without interruption. Moments that hit me hard! Sin and Boyd together again away from the Agency compound had me settling in to read with a big ‘ole grin on my face. Partners sharing opinions and space again. Leaning on each other for support and comfort. Wanting to be there for each other. I adored it! The fountain scene—just the two of them talking—captured everything I love about this series. The banter, looks, warmth and words between these two men never fails to take my breath away. I could feel them sitting there surrounded by the music, noise and energy of the city. It reminded me of Monterrey. It just felt right. Throw in suspense, a guess-that-traitor game, humor, and a cold-hearted bitch…well…I’m a happy woman!<br /><br />For me, Hong Kong also hit on one of my true loves--history. Hong Kong was described as a city stripped of its history due to the war and reconstruction. A city struggling to hold on to its past. History can live and breathe in people’s memories—good or bad they keep history alive. It lives in our heads and hearts. I could feel the city and people of Hong Kong in Sin’s connection to the city and memories as a child. Hsin walking the streets, speaking the language, and looking into the eyes of the young soldiers brought the place and past alive on the page with force and sadness. Hong Kong also felt like the right place for Hsin to tell Boyd certain things. Very powerful part of the story that not only shed light on Sin’s past, but the effects of violence of war on a land and its people--<b>”the idea of not having a choice in the direction your life has turned, of being born into violence and pain.”</b><br /><br /> There are so many reasons why I love this series, but a big one for me is the energy and excitement of new characters. Both authors excel at introducing new voices with humor and mystery. They stand out, live and breathe on the page. Like Xiaolian! She was one unforgettable kick ass bitch! I would give anything to see Sin and Xiaolian battle! Each new mission or adventure brings in new blood and energy adding another layer of fun to the story. Ton (aka Jimmy) was another favorite from Hong Kong. They all leave a mark though. From the cold hearted bitches to the bike rental guy in Vermont—each new character comes to life with quirks and attitude. I love them all!<br /><br />Now I know what you are thinking—Hong Kong, Laura? What about Vermont? Yes, I loved Vermont too! :D How could I not? Shopping. Fucking. Cooking. Relaxing. *sigh* But it was the time in the Jacuzzi that made the whole trip magic for me. That talk in the warm, bubbling water was what I needed to hear. To see Sin stand up for himself, hear Boyd explain and utter certain words made my heart happy, flip and heal. They asked questions, talked and tried so hard to really understand the other side. When Sin and Boyd fuck up---they do it up big with pain and more pain. BUT when they stop, sit down, face each other and finally talk—it is like nothing I’ve experienced before. Powerful, raw, and almost brutal in its intensity. I had such a physical reaction to the words--scrubbing my face, shaking my head, gut twisting, and heart racing. I felt just as naked as they did at that moment. In life and fiction, the big talks and supposed healing moments usually sound the same to me. The same words and actions--“Oh, sorry Babe. I messed up.” But here! Boyd and Sin’s words felt so intense, hard, and true. Even if they walked away still hurt or frustrated, you felt how much they wanted to understand—experienced how much they wanted to forgive and move on. Vermont was one of the most rewarding experiences in my reading life. <br /><br />I feel like this story only gets tighter, more in depth, and heartfelt. The whole cast of characters in and around Hsin and Boyd feel more and more like a family to me. Family and friends trying so hard to survive and gain some control in a dark world filled with danger, betrayal, and treachery.<br /><br />Can’t wait to see what Sonny and Ais have up their sleeves next! Scared, but excited! Both authors are masters of surprise and shock. They have this quiet, off handed way of just blowing my mind! Several times I have had to stop, go back, and ask—did I just read that? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ other son!!!! :o  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Bring it on! Off for more in Fade.<br /><br /><br /><br /><u>My Bitch Fantasy</u><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I so wanted to see Vivienne go head to head with Xiaolian! Haha…I love cold-hearted bitches! I guess because I always wanted to be one. I can’t pull it off though—too much guilt. :D  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /><u>My Laugh Out Loud Moment</u><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I tend to giggle, grin, and smile when I read. A moment truly has to sneak up on me to pull a laugh out of me. Sin got me good during the standoff in the club.<br /><br /><b>“The tranquil scene had been shattered and people were running, cowering behind furniture or foolishly screaming hysterically. Sin’s lips curled in disgust and he wondered how civilians ever got anywhere in life if they acted this ridiculous over a couple of gunshots.”</b> Haha….<br /><br />I can see the eye roll from here! LOL! *shakes head* Assassins! :D  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /><u>My Disappointments</u><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I loved Ivan, but it disappointed me somehow that he looked like Boyd. That robbed some of the emotional impact for me. I didn’t need the physical resemblance to Boyd. No matter what someone looks like—if we close our eyes we will see the ones we lost. The ones we want to love instead. <br /><br /><br />Not enough Ryan. What? I love the little guy. :)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br /><br /><u>Favorite Owen Line</u><br /><br /><b>“Dude, I’ll know whether those sleigh-bells I heard on Christmas morn really came from Santa before I know who’s calling the shots here.”</b><br /><br /><br /><u>Favorite Boyd Line</u><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>“I’m sorry”</b> <br /><br />The word sorry never felt more powerful.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15749122626276730285" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_505357206" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/505357206" />
    <a title="Steph" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4215697-steph"><img alt="Steph" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346102450p2/4215697.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/505357206?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph" href="/user/show/4215697-steph">Steph</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=kindle-read">kindle-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=provided-by-author">provided-by-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer505357206" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer826672507665127414"> <b>Another truly incredible book... *Bows to Sonny and Ais* :)<br/> <br/> I wouldn't read this review, if you haven't atleast read the first two books. I have tried to keep any big spoilers hidden. But I might have missed something. So read ahead at your own risk. LOL <br/><br/> **************************************************************</b><br/><br/><br/> I will admit that this book was really hard on me, emotionally, which I honestly hadn't expected. I really thought that we would see Sin and Boyd be reunited much earlier than the</span>
  <span id="freeText826672507665127414" style="display:none"> <b>Another truly incredible book... *Bows to Sonny and Ais* :)<br /> <br /> I wouldn't read this review, if you haven't atleast read the first two books. I have tried to keep any big spoilers hidden. But I might have missed something. So read ahead at your own risk. LOL <br /><br /> **************************************************************</b><br /><br /><br /> I will admit that this book was really hard on me, emotionally, which I honestly hadn't expected. I really thought that we would see Sin and Boyd be reunited much earlier than they were. I was so desperate for them to be back together, that I held my breath through every scene between them, every word and every little look or touch. <br /> Seeing Boyd and Sin apart was so difficult to take, even though I knew when they split up that it was for the best. They needed to learn how to be strong alone before they can be any good together, but that doesn’t make it any easier, unfortunately.<br /><br /> <b>
  <i>"All I know is that I don’t want to not see you, even if all it amounts to is awkwardness. And I know I still want to touch you, even though you don’t want me to anymore."</i>
</b><br /><br /> One of the things I really adored about this book; was watching Sin grow, seeing him make friends and become more comfortable with himself as a person. But most of all, it was seeing him discover his own feelings. Deciding what he actually felt, now that he wasn’t dependant on Boyd for stability…<br /><br /> <i>
  <b>"It doesn’t change that I still want him, I still want to be with him, I still feel like the fucking air has been sucked out of the room when he walks in and I still think about him all the time."</b>
</i><br /> <br /> His brutal honesty definitely comes from his father. I literally spat out my tea whilst reading this part, he’s so damn funny…<br /> <br /> '<i><b>"I do not understand why men do such things."</b><br /> Growing irritated by the pointless discussion, Sin sneered. <b>"Maybe you should try it sometime and then decide. You might enjoy having your cock stuffed in a tight ass."</b><br /> Bo-Qin’s thoughtful expression slid into a dark glare and he turned away, leaving the room as abruptly as he entered.'</i><br /> Bwahahaha.<br /><br />Onto some of the secondary characters.<br /><br /> <u>Ivan:</u><br /> I was so confused by Ivan’s presence. One minute I was so happy that Sin had someone to talk to again. The next, I felt like he was stopping Sin and Boyd from making the progress that was needed between them. <br /> He seemed like such a nice guy though, he was there for Sin when he needed a friend and to show him that not only Boyd thinks he’s an amazing person. I think Sin really needed that…<br /><br /> <i>
  <b>"It’s just that you’re truly, honestly, breathtakingly gorgeous, Hsin. It’s difficult for me to ignore as it is but when you smile like that it’s impossible. Your entire face lights up. It’s very striking."</b>
</i><br /><br /> As I mentioned in my review of Afterimage, I was already falling in love with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emilio, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <i>(I’m hiding his name just in case, don’t want to spoil anything for others)</i> before we even really knew him, his brutal honesty sucked me in from the get go. Yes, he’s rude and disgusting, a real asshole too. <b>But my God do I love him.</b> He’s so much fun. I think that out of everyone, it’s his relationship with Boyd that intrigued me, and made me laugh the most. It was so easy to forget that he is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sin’s father <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> because 90% of the time, he didn’t act like it. He was so pervy about Boyd and Sin together, and constantly propositioning Boyd, it was hilarious. If not a little creepy! LOL.<br /><br /><i>'……'s mouth twitched up slightly but then he just shrugged exaggeratedly and said slowly, <b>"Or maybe… you just think I’m cute. Admit it, Boyd. Don’t deny your true feelings anymore. It’s mean to be – you, me, my boy… How would you like to be in the middle of a Vega sandwich?"</b></i>'<br /> Bwahahaha.<br /> Boyd and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emilio <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> work so well together. There’s something about their personalities that just <i>click</i>. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emilio <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> opens up to him about things I never would have expected him to say out loud and I like that he has someone to talk to, I don’t think he has anyone else. I like that Boyd recognises that.<br /><br /> '<i><b>"Sometimes,"</b>…… said in a low dangerous voice. <b>"Sometimes I get so fucking angry I just imagine myself killing him. That’s how crazy he drives me. Sometimes I just want him to fuckin die so I won’t be like this no more."<br /> "If that ever happened you’d regret it far more than anything in the end."</b> Boyd replied calmly.<br /><b>"Yeah,"</b> ...... agreed quietly, nodding seriously in response. <b>"I’d probably blow my own brains out after. Maybe that wouldn’t be so bad though…"</b></i>'<br /><br /> The poor guy is in such a mess. He has no idea how to be normal, how to go about his feelings. It’s hard to see. I really hope things get better for him in the next book.<br /><br /> Now onto <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emilio and Carhart(Zach) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Wow, where to start. Their relationship is so frickin complicated. <br /> You can tell from the very start that something has happened between them in the past. They were very close before their twenty year separation and it was obvious that their differences are hurting <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emilio <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, he wants the old Zach back.<br /> I liked how they behaved towards each other, that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emilio <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was never bothered by Zachary’s new status as a General. He was still as honest as ever, and treated Zach the same as he always did.<br /><br /> I still love Kassian, just as much as before. But we definitely got to see a different side to him in this book. We learned so much more about his past, what he has had to suffer through, at the hands of the Agency, and the damage it has done to his life. I was so horrified by some of what we saw, it’s really not surprising he is drinking so badly. <br /><br /> Vivienne is on par, being a total bitch as usual. Nothing new there! LOL. If I get started on this lady, I will never stop. So I am moving on :)<br /><br /> I found this book a lot harder to read, than Afterimage. I found Sin and Boyd being so sweet and nice to each other, without being a couple, unbearable. I would have preferred shouting and screaming to this. Having to watch each other with different people was awful, and fearing that they might never be together again? <i>*shudders*</i> I never want to see them like that again.<br /> All the angst and separation was so worth it in the end. Boyd and Sin’s reunion was more than I could’ve hoped for. I was crying very happy tears :)<br /> <br /> <i>'His gaze was intense and sincere as he didn’t look away from Sin’s eyes. <b>"I love you more than I’ve ever loved anyone. I think about you all the time. It’s been hell trying to keep myself away – every time you’re close I just want to touch you. I would do anything for you. <br /> And if I could have anything in the world right now, I would be in a relationship with you."</b>'</i><br /><br /> One of my favourite scenes was at Kassian’s pool party, I loved the group banter. <br /> <br /> '<i><b>"Some field agents actually spend their free time reading, and not being lazy fat assess playing video games and chugging beer."</b><br /> There was a brief silence and Ryan looked on the verge of pissing himself with laughter although he managed to keep it in.<br /> <b>"I’m not a fat ass,"</b> Kassian said icily.<br /> <b>"Not yet…"<br /> "You eat fucking donuts for dinner on missions!"</b> Kassian practically shouted incredulously.'</i><br /> Bwahahaha.<br /> <br /> But the best scenes EVER, were in Vermont. <b>Vermont is definitely the new Mexico.</b> You all know what I’m talking about *wink wink*.<br /> <br /> I have to end this review by saying that I am terrified. I know it seems a little crazy because I loved this book so much, but the last three or four per cent really made me nervous. I just have to hope that something comes up, before Boyd can go on this mission? Surely it can’t go ahead, it just can’t! Everything was going so well, I am scared of what this will do to them all over again.<br /> Also, the person responsible for the Raid on the Agency was revealed. I could not believe it, and the way it all slotted in together was so perfect. Amazing writing!<br /> <b>Although I am shitting myself, worrying about Fade, I cannot wait to start. Yes, I am a total glutton for punishment. LOL</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="826672507665127414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2048503084" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2048503084" />
    <a title="Virginia Cavanillas" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19380470-virginia-cavanillas"><img alt="Virginia Cavanillas" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1556819327p2/19380470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2048503084?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Cavanillas" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Cavanillas" href="/user/show/19380470-virginia-cavanillas">Virginia Cavanillas</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19380470-virginia-cavanillas?shelf=lgtb">lgtb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19380470-virginia-cavanillas?shelf=rambles">rambles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19380470-virginia-cavanillas?shelf=sci-fi-romance">sci-fi-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2048503084" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18127877779567692987">Rating removed because of this:<br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statement-on-sh'>http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statem...</a><br/><br/>I still admire Ais tho <br/><br/>Original review:<br/><br/><strong>This book is the ultimate material for fangirling</strong>. We are talking serious here. The characters, quotes and situations are destined to fangirl, sigh, smile, laugh, cry and give the reader goosebumps. Or at least, that was what I experienced while reading The Interludes.<br/>Because, let me tell you just a little thing: this book is fantastic, addictive and, as it's predecessors, masterfully wr</span>
  <span id="freeText18127877779567692987" style="display:none">Rating removed because of this:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statement-on-sh">http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statem...</a><br><br>I still admire Ais tho <br><br>Original review:<br><br><strong>This book is the ultimate material for fangirling</strong>. We are talking serious here. The characters, quotes and situations are destined to fangirl, sigh, smile, laugh, cry and give the reader goosebumps. Or at least, that was what I experienced while reading The Interludes.<br>Because, let me tell you just a little thing: this book is fantastic, addictive and, as it's predecessors, masterfully written.<br>Santino &amp; Ais keep amazing me and I'm a super happy reader right now.<strong> I'm a fan. A huge one with heart eyes and a smile in my face</strong>, even if the path hasn't been a sweet and peaceful one. On the contrary, it has been long, hard and sometimes, cruel.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1501432192i/23458063.jpg" width="322" height="181" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Detailed and developed to the maximum in a flawless way (even if some parts were too long for my tastes), book three in the ICoS series<strong> is easier to read than Afterimage</strong> and it's also<strong> more exciting and powerful. Less sad (Hsin related) and less painful</strong>.<br><br><em>
  <strong>"I just don´t know what the fuck to do. I don´t know how to move on and I dont know if I even want to"</strong>
</em> (Hsin)<br><br>It has a lot of mixed genres.<strong> The love story is still our base</strong> (sad and complicated but for the first time: hopeful). <strong>The sci-fi our frame</strong> (world building to die for) and the <strong>thriller and the mystery</strong>, a big part of it (pure entertainment perfectly executed).<br>Also this one is much dirtier than the others, and much more dynamic probably because of the different POVs used.<br>And that's the thing, <strong>the multiple POVs was a total hit. Superb</strong>. This book is full of amazing characters creating subplots by themselves. Stories that you want to follow and not only because you know they are converging in your ending. No. You want to read them because they are perfect, entertaining, developed and very interesting.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1501432192i/23458064._SY540_.jpg" width="290" height="436" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I don't want to slaughter the plot revealing any details. So <strong>I'm just going to spit my thoughts</strong> as usual and even that its gonna be difficult this time  because <strong> I have a lot of feelings right now. A lot of messed up thoughts</strong> that I can't (and I won't) write up. If I'd try it would be boringly long and complicated to follow since I've been taking notes, and filling pages about everything that happened (and how it affected me). Now it's difficult to summarize without being extremely detailed, so I won't try and I'm just gonna say a few things (maybe still a lot, but that's life)<br><br>First and most important thought:<strong> I love Hsin Liu Vega</strong> and I reaffirm myself declaring him as one of the most attractive characters ever written. Here he blooms and it is beautiful to watch.<br><br><em>
  <strong>"I still want to be with him, I still feel like the fucking air has been sucked out of the room when he walks in and I still think about him all the time" </strong>
</em>(Says Hsin)<br><br>Second main feeling: <strong>Boyd's evolution is huge</strong>. His character development is impressive and so is the way the authors show us why and how he changes. Boyd grows before the reader's eyes.<strong> I love you, blondie</strong>, you've given me wonderful moments, hair-raising quotes and some well deserved tears.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1501432192i/23458065.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>
  <em>"I love you more than I ever love anyone. I think about you all the time. It´s been hell trying to keep myself away- everytime you are close I just want to touch you-. I would do anything for you. And if I could have anything in the world right now, I would be in a relationship with you"</em>
</strong> (Boyd to Hsin)<br><br>Third thing to highlight: Even if I think <strong>some of the missions were a bit too much</strong> (too long, too detailed...) all of them served their purpose: to get to know the character more deeply and, of course, to get some good action.<br><br>And my fourth thought goes to: <strong>The side characters. They are the bomb</strong>. Every single one of them. The ones you knew, and the new additions. The ones you love, the ones you just like or dislike, and the ones you hate. All of them are complex and perfectly structured. You understand their motivations. Awesome work here. And, of course, I have my special mention in this regard <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<strong>Emiliooooooooo I love youuuuuuu</strong>!<br>What an asshole. What a hot, funny and entertaining piece of shit. <strong>Te quiero, Emilio</strong>. I wanted to make a love letter just for you but, well, you have a son and I love him more than I love you, so it wasn't fair. That´s the only reason I'm not embarrassing myself with an ode just for you and your sexy and sarcastic bones. But I need, at least, to quote you<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1501432192i/23458066.jpg" width="287" height="223" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And to quote your wise and marvelous son:<br><br><em><strong>"And you say I´m the one with a blonde obsession"</strong></em><br><br>Awesome and super welcome character. <br>And Emilio and Zachary? Hell yeah, I want more! Much more! Another hit from Santino &amp; Ais and one perfectly aimed. How happy I am with this couple. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><strong>This one has it all</strong>: love, mystery, delicious bickering, deep conversations, fantastic sex scenes (role playing included. Yay!) and a lot of action. And I insist about the world building, because it is wonderful and a delight to sci-fi fans.<br>A highly recommend series, even if the Director´s cut is gonna be better.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501432192ra/23458067.gif" width="397" height="387" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><em><strong>Note to readers</strong>: This is book 3 in a series. Can't be read as standalone.</em><br><em>Also, I kept my review spoiler free but the comments below contain spoilers, so be careful reading them, please! It's for your own good! You don't want to know, believe me. Not yet.</em></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText3329282485663246882" style="display:none">This one was even better than Afterimage! Despite being so long it was more fast-paced but definitely not less intense.   <span id="freeText11529362336357402509" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS!!!</b><br /><br /><br />The word "WOW" to me has never been so inadequate to describe something awesome.. Until now.<br /><br />This is a serious masterpiece right here!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>And i don't have any delusion that I could come up with anything closely related to describing how much of a great book this is. </i>
</b><br /><br />A lot had happened and I have enjoyed every hours, minutes down to the every seconds of it. I have a lot of unread book stashed in my shelf right now.. But I couldn't give a flying f**** as long as I'm with Sin and Boyd.<br /><br />It has achieved many many things for me. And yes! Thats including me forgiving Boyd whom I thought to be the shittiest character I've ever met. And believe me when I say no other character have ever riled me up like he did before.. But now? Man, I thoroughly love everything about him. Yes, that includes his past mistakes. That alone is a testament how tremendously well Santino and Ais could write their asses off.<br /><br />This book put my heart back together after it being shattered everywhere from the previous installment. It was just so..satisfying.<br /><br />And man.. I got no other words. I can't prolong writing this nonsense review because I'm totally itching to read the next with that kind of a bomb ending.<br /><br />But.. Fade, pleaase be careful with my heart. I've heard from people that you are the most badass heartbreaker among the series. But please, please, please.. I only ask you this: put it back together, 'kay?</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2195749470" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16828046265215305709"><blockquote>
  <b>"How would you like to be in the middle of a Vega sandwich?"</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1511725458i/24538248._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yep, that quote marked my life. #SorryNotSorry<br/><br/>This book was delicious, there isn't any other way for me to describe it.<br/><br/>Yes, it was a rollercoaster of emotion, but omg Hsin and Boyd.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401981450ra/9877278.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I'm so proud of <b>Boyd</b>, he certainly went through a change in this book. Nothing too big to make it feel unbelievable, but it was significant enough for you to see that he isn't the same selfish brat he was since book one. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"I live you more than I've eve</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16828046265215305709" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"How would you like to be in the middle of a Vega sandwich?"</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1511725458i/24538248._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yep, that quote marked my life. #SorryNotSorry<br><br>This book was delicious, there isn't any other way for me to describe it.<br><br>Yes, it was a rollercoaster of emotion, but omg Hsin and Boyd.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401981450ra/9877278.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'm so proud of <b>Boyd</b>, he certainly went through a change in this book. Nothing too big to make it feel unbelievable, but it was significant enough for you to see that he isn't the same selfish brat he was since book one. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I live you more than I've ever loved anyone. I think about you all the time. It's been hell trying to keep myself away- every time you're close I just want to touch you. I would do anything for you. And if I could have anything in the world right now, I would be in a relationship with you."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>He loves Hsin, he has his priorities well established now and that's all that matters to me. <br><br><b>Hsin, my baby.</b> He's still amazing in everything he does, he's not suffering so much anymore and he's crazy in love with his little blond.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"It doesn't change that I still want him, I still want to be with him, I still feel like the fucking air has been sucked out of the room when he walks in and I still think about him all the time."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Interludes felt totally different from the other books, I don't know if it was due to the change that the characters underwent but even Hsin and Boyd's relationship felt different. It was more intense, honest and hotter. Gez, they wanted to be just like in Monterrey but I feel like this time is way better than anything they had before! <br><br>And omg, I laughed so hard with Hsin. His sarcasm and his witty crack me up. It's good to know that those kinds of stuff were genetically inherited ;). <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I have occasional nightmares about us having a threesome with that meat-head. I'm far from being easily shocked."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>(For him was a nightmare, for me is something I need in real action now.)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1511725433i/24538247.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>PERFECT! Even better than Afterimages. Can't wait for Fade, but I don't want this series to be over so I'm stalling :(.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3668273202495908059">Interludes was definitely the toughest book of the series to get through and like many people have said, I was hoping that Boyd and Sin would get back together for a large part of the book. It was torturous seeing them separated and tiptoeing around each other, not wanting to offend or say the wrong thing.   <span id="freeText3668273202495908059" style="display:none">Interludes was definitely the toughest book of the series to get through and like many people have said, I was hoping that Boyd and Sin would get back together for a large part of the book. It was torturous seeing them separated and tiptoeing around each other, not wanting to offend or say the wrong thing. I was just waiting for a glimmer of hope that things would be fine. <br /><br />However, after reaching the end of the book I now realize that Boyd and Sin needed the time apart to really appreciate how much they loved each other and to understand exactly what kind of a relationship they wanted.<br />They needed space.<br /><br />I breathed a sigh of relief at the end of the book knowing that Boyd and Sin were still together and I'm keeping my fingers crossed that things will stay that way.<br /></span>

<div id="review_1201260619" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1201260619" />
    <a title="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15615404-tara-mindforbooks"><img alt="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1547115831p2/15615404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1201260619?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" href="/user/show/15615404-tara-mindforbooks">Tara♥ {MindforBooks}</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=epic-covers">epic-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=2015-books">2015-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=heroes-i-love">heroes-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=lickable-males">lickable-males</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=favourites-2015">favourites-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1201260619" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15193283997830976029"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425317893ra/13876403.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Without a doubt this one is my favourite of the series so far. While reading it I just could not get over how far both Hsin and Boyd have come. I adored Monterrey and all that happened there but I was always a little uneasy about how intense their relationship was throughout that period, mostly because as is their way the lack of communication meant that neither of them was truly sure where they stood. <br/><br/>I don’t think I have ever questioned the fact that these two love each other, it was always s</span>
  <span id="freeText15193283997830976029" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425317893ra/13876403.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Without a doubt this one is my favourite of the series so far. While reading it I just could not get over how far both Hsin and Boyd have come. I adored Monterrey and all that happened there but I was always a little uneasy about how intense their relationship was throughout that period, mostly because as is their way the lack of communication meant that neither of them was truly sure where they stood. <br><br>I don’t think I have ever questioned the fact that these two love each other, it was always so very clear that they had something incredibly special but I think the biggest problem for them both was that neither truly understood what was expected of them. Sin had absolutely no idea how to navigate a personal relationship, he had no experience with them, and everything that Sin does in terms of human interaction seems to be guess work. Boyd also as far as I could see had very little idea on the workings of a functional relationship. (I mean seriously, look at the women who birthed him.) Lou was his only real experience and he was so young at the time that I’m not sure it can be compared to what he has with Sin, even when they both met Boyd was still so young, I do think that he needed that time apart to grow, to come into himself while not under a cloud of depression. Just like I think Sin needed that time apart from Boyd when he was being treated for his illness and living a life outside of ‘The Box’ and participating somewhat in society. They both needed each other at the start so that they could start living life but they also needed the time they spent apart so that they could discover who they really were, once that started to happen, once they were both healthy and somewhat at peace? WOW!!! <br><br><b> “It doesn't change that I still want him, I still want to be with him, I still feel like the fucking air has been sucked out of the room when he walks in and I still think about him all the time.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425317893ra/13876404.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"Sin was more important to him than anything or anyone else and he would gladly give up his life for the opportunity to try to protect and save him."</b><br><br>Monterrey will always be special but the time the boys spent in Vermont was just the absolute business. Vermont is my new favourite. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425317893i/13876405.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But it also has made me kind of sad. Sad because it really was very beautiful to witness them both away from The Agency and the pressure that is their everyday life. I’m very worried about what is to come now. I’m worried about the new administration and I’m worried about what Sin and Boyd are about to go through. The little bit of peace seemed too good to be true while it was happening and unfortunately that proved to be the case. <br><br><b>”He wanted to say something more. That he wouldn't have wanted to spend the time any other way. That whatever else he'd have been doing didn't matter. That Boyd meant more to him than anything else in existence. That Sin never wanted him to leave the bed. That he never wanted to let him go into the uncertainties of tomorrow.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425317893ra/13876406.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"Things never work out for us. It's always the calm before the storm. Maybe it will always be this way until we finally fucking die in this place."</b><br><br>Outside forces have always caused these two the most pain and as long as they can weather the storms that those forces bring I think that they will be okay. I’m just not looking forward to those storms though. I’m terrified if I’m honest. <br><br>The Interludes also brought us the force of nature that is Emilio Vega. Emilio is just one of the most amazing characters I have ever come across. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410524ra/805076.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>No matter what way I look at it I’m pretty sure that I should hate him but I just couldn’t. In fact I’m pretty sure I’m in love with him. Boyd and Kassian actually discussed the Emilio effect. <br><br><b>"I don't understand it. I hated him before I met him because of what I thought he'd done to Hsin. I love Hsin; I'll always side with him. Yet when I met Emilio it was hard to hate him the way I had before. He's come onto me a few times, even twice bringing up a ridiculous idea of a threesome with Hsin--"<br> <br>He shook his head to himself and made a face.<br> <br>"You'd think I'd dismiss it entirely like I would with anyone else but something about that damn man makes the question stick in the back of my head. I tell myself I'm only intrigued because he looks so much like Hsin but who knows, maybe it's just his charm."<br> <br>"It's got to be," Kassian muttered, looking irritated by it. "Bastard."</b> <br><br>That charm hops off the page it really does. No matter what fucked up or crazy shit he does I found myself forgiving him. There is an incident with Carhart that was just not okay and I ended up feeling sorry for him at the end of it all. HOW IS THAT EVEN POSSIBLE? It’s absolute madness. I will say one thing though, I agree with him on one point. Carhart is totally messing with his head.<br><br><b>”You even have commitment issues with criminal activities”</b><br><br>Yet again at the end of The Interludes I have no answers. Yet again I have only questions. I know I’m in for some pain. I know the next 1200 pages are going to be a rollercoaster. But I do think that at the end, the people who need to know will know that:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425317893i/13876407.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15193283997830976029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15586992633310838767"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Might contain spoilers*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/>Though this book was better than the previous one, I still ended up feeling frustrated throughout the whole book. <b>Hsin ‘Sin’ Liu Vega</b> (27?) and <b>Boyd Kadin Beaulieu</b> (22/23?) finally got truthful with each other, and we got a nice relationship I had wanted from the start, however, something always comes along and want to destroy it/shake it up. Although, Hsin and Boyd opening up to each other took forever, it still happened. There was too much of <b>Kassian Eri</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15586992633310838767" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Might contain spoilers*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br />Though this book was better than the previous one, I still ended up feeling frustrated throughout the whole book. <b>Hsin ‘Sin’ Liu Vega</b> (27?) and <b>Boyd Kadin Beaulieu</b> (22/23?) finally got truthful with each other, and we got a nice relationship I had wanted from the start, however, something always comes along and want to destroy it/shake it up. Although, Hsin and Boyd opening up to each other took forever, it still happened. There was too much of <b>Kassian Eric Trovosky</b> (early thirties?) in this book, which annoyed me. In book one and half of book two, Kassian interested me, but now, for me, he's become a disliked person. <b>Vivienne Amarante Beaulieu</b> (38), I hope you get what's coming for you (I really hope something <i>is</i> coming for her) after how you treat your son and his lover. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“So... why did it end?”<br />Sin looked at Boyd sidelong before shrugging simply. “Because he wasn't you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b>Zachary Andrew Carhart</b> (43) and <b>Emilio Vega</b> (42?) was unhealthy for each other, but somehow I wanted them to be a couple... which was strange because I don't like Emilio at all because of his attitude and I felt like we didn't <i>really</i> get to know him. Carhart I also didn't like; he's too cold with a stick up his ass. Overall the story was boring for the most part, things got better when things started to work out for Hsin and Boyd but I disliked the ending and I still hate Boyd's <i>valentine</i> job. I hate cliffhangers. But I only got one left, right? Now I just want to finish this series and I seriously hope I get that happy ending I've been waiting for. And I fucking want that fucking Agency destroyed!<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Stop looking at me like you want to fuck me.”<br />Emilio's expression didn't change but once again he swallowed thickly, shifting and absently curling his hands into fists. “But I do want to fuck you.”</i>
  </b>

<span id="freeTextContainer11940111827801840088">Since I started reading this series, I've felt so many different emotions, some not very good and others absolutely fabulous... But I must say that, after reading Afterimage, I was scared about what could possibly happen next! And to be honest, I still don't know very well what to feel about this book... It is amazing, captivating and with so many mysteries, that is impossible not want to know more! I hated the beginning, felt so much frustration, that it looked like Afterimage 2... but then thi</span>
  <span id="freeText11940111827801840088" style="display:none">Since I started reading this series, I've felt so many different emotions, some not very good and others absolutely fabulous... But I must say that, after reading Afterimage, I was scared about what could possibly happen next! And to be honest, I still don't know very well what to feel about this book... It is amazing, captivating and with so many mysteries, that is impossible not want to know more! I hated the beginning, felt so much frustration, that it looked like Afterimage 2... but then things started to get better. That pause in Hsin and Boyd's relationship actually was good for them, and it was fantastic to watch the growth of trust, of friendship and mostly, the confirmation of a beautiful love! <br><br><a href="http://s1296.photobucket.com/user/igrilo/media/M_M/giphy1_zps6f7ab700.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>Vermont and a cabin... what a perfect combination! There are no words to describe the Vermont scenes... sex, kisses, tenderness... *sigh*...<br><br><br><a href="http://s1296.photobucket.com/user/igrilo/media/6c2240f2-8a66-4834-83e1-85f5462f609d_zpsc622a584.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>And then... then that ending... I don't Boyd to go... that sounds so wrong! It was really a mood killer, and now I'm worried again with what more is going to happen... So, you see, it is very difficult to say what to feel about such a complex and fantastic book!<br><br>One final note: I love Vega men(father and son)!!!<br><br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText9317032024261977694" style="display:none">Rating removed!<br><br>I never thought it would be possible, but I love this series even more with each new book!!! <br><br>Even if it is bordering sometimes at being almost unbearable and even if it <b>is</b> reeaaalllly long, it doesn't feel this way and not once I felt the need to read another book in between. If anything, as for me this series could go on forever and I'm already dreading the day when it comes to an end.<br><br>Whereas the previous book did concentrate a lot on feelings, The Interludes had me almost constantly on the edge of my seat, because one assignment followed the other. And even if there was no mission, there were enough either creepy or emotional situations which kept me riveted. <br><br>The Interludes was a bit different from the previous books. There was a variety of perspektives, but that's exactly what did provide further insight and I loved it.<br><br>And finally, FINALLY(!!!), Sin and Boyd were back on track with their feelings for each other! How long did I have to wait for this...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463148920i/19087030._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463159252i/19088755._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As for the ending... <span id="freeTextContainer13591767839243027108">Only for Ais...<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>And here we are again. ICoS is one of the best series that I've read.<br/>It's amazing what these books do to me. Wich exceptionally strong emotions these cause.<br/>I was angry, desperate, perished with fear, have suffered, scolded, laughed and cried ... sometimes at the same time. I feel like wrung out. Emotional completely exhausted. Is that not crazy?<br/><br/>But there is that hateful agency:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469104930i/19780511._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My Boyd. Whom I love and sometimes wanted to strangle. He has become incredibly fast really grown up. Pru</span>
  <span id="freeText13591767839243027108" style="display:none">Only for Ais...<br><br><br><br><br><br>And here we are again. ICoS is one of the best series that I've read.<br>It's amazing what these books do to me. Wich exceptionally strong emotions these cause.<br>I was angry, desperate, perished with fear, have suffered, scolded, laughed and cried ... sometimes at the same time. I feel like wrung out. Emotional completely exhausted. Is that not crazy?<br><br>But there is that hateful agency:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469104930i/19780511._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My Boyd. Whom I love and sometimes wanted to strangle. He has become incredibly fast really grown up. Prudently and soulful, thoughtful and a wonderful partner and lover.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469104930i/19780512._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sin was as always to fall in love. And the man has remade me terrible worries. As always, too.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469104930i/19780513._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Great supporting characters:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469104930i/19780514._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469104930i/19780515._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469104930i/19780516._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emilio's humor was often the only thing that saved me from a nervous breakdown.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469104930i/19780517._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://youtu.be/N1Whs15WSyM" rel="nofollow noopener">And when words are not enough ... look here</a><br><br><a href="https://youtu.be/SB2PSzqgtro" rel="nofollow noopener">and here ...</a><br><br>And on it goes with Fade. I hope someone is holding my hand. I'm so afraid ...</span>
